The **greatest human principle** (*dà lún*) is called **governance** (*zhì*).
What **governance** (*zhì*) **relies upon** (*yīn*) is called **division** (*bì*).

**Exalting** (*chóng*) **Heaven** (*tiān*) and **universal** (*pǔ*) **Earth** (*dì*), **partitioning** (*fèn*) **groups** (*qún*) and **paired** (*ǒu*) **things** (*wù*), **making** (*shǐ*) them **not lose** (*bù shī*) their **order** (*tǒng*)—
none **more effective** (*mó ruò*) than **division** (*bì*).

**Heaven** (*tiān*) **divides** (*bì*) from the **upper** (*shàng*), **Earth** (*dì*) **divides** (*bì*) from the **lower** (*xià*), the **Sovereign** (*jūn*) **divides** (*bì*) from the **center** (*zhōng*).

**Gazing upward** (*yǎng tiān*) at **Heaven** (*tiān*), yet **Heaven** (*tiān*) does not **weary** (*qì*)—
*qì* and *qì* are the same.
**Gazing downward** (*fǔ dì*) at **Earth** (*dì*), yet **Earth** (*dì*) does not **be idle** (*dài*).
**Weary** (*qì*) not **Heaven** (*tiān*), **idle** (*dài*) not **Earth** (*dì*).
**Weary** (*qì*) and **idle** (*dài*), yet **able** (*néng*) in **their affairs** (*shì*)—
ancient and modern **none** (*wèi*) have **marked** (*zhǔ*) this.

Thus, the **Sage** (*shèng rén*) **upholds** (*áng*) **Heaven** (*tiān*) and is **constant** (*cháng*).
**Exhausts** (*qióng*) the **divine** (*shén*), **digs** (*jué*) **transformation** (*biàn*).
**Extremes** (*jí*) **things** (*wù*), **exhausts** (*qióng*) **sentiment** (*qíng*).

**Aligns** (*pèi*) with **Heaven** (*tiān*) and **Earth** (*dì*) in **their forms** (*tǐ*), **with spirits** (*guǐ*) and **gods** (*shén*) in **their essences** (*líng*), **with yin** (*yīn*) and **yang** (*yáng*) in **their transformations** (*huà*), **with the Four Seasons** (*sì shí*) in **their sincerity** (*chéng*).
**Views** (*shì*) **Heaven** (*tiān*) and **Heaven** (*tiān*) **obeys** (*xún*), **views** (*shì*) **Earth** (*dì*) and **Earth** (*dì*) **obeys** (*xún*), **views** (*shì*) the **divine** (*shén*) and the **divine** (*shén*) **obeys** (*xún*), **views** (*shì*) **times** (*shí*) and **times** (*shí*) **obey** (*xún*).
**Heaven** (*tiān*), **Earth** (*dì*), **divine** (*shén*), and **times** (*shí*) all **submissive** (*xún*), yet **evil** (*è*) **enters** (*rù*) **rebellion** (*nì*)?

The *Poem* (*Shī*) says:
*"The august Sovereign maintains **division** (*bì*), **law triumphs** (*fǎ shèng*).*
**Central** (*zhōng*) is the **virtue** (*dé*) of the **Sovereign** (*jūn*), yet **division** (*bì*) **governs** (*tǒng*) **uprightness** (*zhèng*).
This is what is called **Great Beginning** (*tài shǐ*), from which the **transformations** (*yùn*) of **Heaven** (*tiān*) and **Earth** (*dì*) **commence** (*qǐ*).

**Mystery** (*xuán*) **praise** (*zàn*) **research** (*yán*), **commence** (*qǐ*), **cut** (*qiè*).
**Praise** (*zàn*) of **mystery** (*xuán*), sometimes **with qi** (*qì*), sometimes **with kindred** (*lèi*), sometimes **with affairs** (*shì*) **in their** (*zhī*) **exhaustion** (*jué*).

**Exhaustion** (*jué*), pronounced as *wěi*.
**Examine** (*jiǎn*) **its surname** (*xìng*), **investigate** (*shěn*) **its family** (*jiā*).
**Observe** (*guàn*) **its encounters** (*zāo yù*), **labor** (*lè*)—
**its affairs** (*shì*), **detailed** (*xiáng*) in **numbers** (*shù*).
**Meeting** (*féng*) the **divine** (*shén*), **Heaven** (*tiān*) **obeys** (*xún*).
**Touching** (*chù*) **Earth** (*dì*), **fields** (*tián*) **obey** (*xún*).
Then the **sentiment** (*qíng*) of **mystery** (*xuán*) is **obtained** (*dé*).

Thus, **head** (*shǒu*) is **Heavenly nature** (*tiān xìng*).
**Chōng** (*chōng*), **opposite** (*duì*) its **uprightness** (*zhèng*).
**Cuò** (*cuò*), **interwoven** (*jiā*).
*Cuò* (*cuò*), pronounced as *bìng* or *bìng* (普耕切).

**Yuan** (*yuán*), **patterns** (*wén*) **and** (*guǐ*) **ornaments** (*qǐ*), **mixed** (*zá*).
**Measure** (*cè*), **by which** (*suǒ*) **to know** (*zhī*) its **sentiment** (*qíng*).
**Zhān** (*zhān*), **to extend** (*zhāng*).
**Yíng** (*yíng*), **to illuminate** (*míng*).

**Numbers** (*shù*) for **categories** (*pǐn*) and **patterns** (*shì*), **ornaments** (*wén*) for **adornment** (*zǎo shì*).
**Qiè** (*qiè*), **to imitate** (*nǐ*).
**Tú** (*tú*), **to symbolize** (*xiàng*).
**Gào** (*gào*), **its path** (*yú*) **of departure** (*wǎng*).

**Heaven** (*tiān*) **first bestows** (*zào jiàng*) **life** (*shēng*) upon **the people** (*mín*), **making** (*shǐ*) their **appearance** (*mào*) **move** (*dòng*), **mouths** (*kǒu*) **speak** (*yán*), **eyes** (*mù*) **see** (*shì*), **ears** (*ěr*) **listen** (*tīng*), **hearts** (*xīn*) **think** (*sī*).
**There are laws** (*yǒu fǎ*), then **formation** (*chéng*) occurs.
**There are no laws** (*wú fǎ*), then **formation** (*chéng*) does not occur.

**Sincerity** (*chéng*) **has** (*yǒu*) **not-sincerity** (*bù chéng*), *Fàn* and *Sòng* read as *"sincerity has no awe"* (*bù wēi*), *Dīng* reads as *"not fear"* (*bù xìng*), *Huáng* reads as *"not-sincerity"* (*bù chéng*).
**Imitation** (*qiè nǐ*) **of laws** (*jīng*).

**Cloth** (*yī*) as **garment** (*yī*), **lapel** (*rèn*)—
*rèn* pronounced as *shān* (所交切).
**Skirt** (*cháng*) **with folds** (*zhé*) **and** (*fú*) **width** (*fú*).
*zhé* pronounced as *bì* (音壁).

The **garment** (*yī*) and **skirt** (*cháng*) **institution** (*zhì*), all **originals** (*zhū běn*) read as *"institution"* (*zhì*), *Sòng* only says *"garment and skirt"* (*yī cháng*) **institutes** (*zhì*) **the world** (*shì tiān xià*).
Nearly **original** (*jìn běn*) reads as *"institution"* (*zhì*).
**To institute** (*zhì*) **the world** (*tiān xià*), **imitation** (*qiè nǐ*) **of laws** (*jīng*) **in the** (*zhī*) **Eight** (*sān bā*).

**Strips** (*bǐ*) **of** (*zhé*) **writing** (*zá*) as **armor** (*jiǎ*), **hat** (*guàn*) **of** (*jūn*) **pride** (*qiāo*) as **spear** (*jǐ*).
**Wearing armor** (*bèi jiǎ*) **and** (*hé*) **spear** (*jǐ*), **pride** (*qiāo*)—
*jūn* pronounced as *jù* (巨巾切), **spear shaft** (*máo dǐng*).

**To threaten** (*wēi*) **without reverence** (*bù kè*), **imitation** (*qiè nǐ*) **of laws** (*jīng*) **in the** (*zhī*) **Four** (*sì*) **Nine** (*jiǔ*).

**Respectful** (*zūn*) **respectful** (*zūn*) as **Sovereign** (*jūn*), **low** (*bēi*) **low** (*bēi*) as **minister** (*chén*).
The **Sovereign** (*jūn*) and **minister** (*chén*) **institution** (*zhì*), **upper** (*shàng*) and **lower** (*xià*) **with boundaries** (*jiè*).
**Imitation** (*qiè nǐ*) **of laws** (*jīng*) **in the** (*zhī*) **

The **ghosts and spirits** (*guǐshén*) **waste and ravage** (*hàohuāng*), **their forms** (*xiǎng*) **are without** (*wú*) **boundaries** (*fāng*).
They **know no winter nor summer** (*wú dōng wú xià*), **their sacrifices** (*jì*) **are without measure** (*wú dù*).
Thus, the **Sage** (*shèngrén*) **established** (*zhuó*) **them with rites** (*sìdiǎn*), **imitation** (*qiè nǐ*) **of the** (*zhī*) **One** (*yī*) **Six** (*liù*).

**Timing the heavens** (*shí tiān*), **strengthening the earth** (*lì dì*).
**The five grains** (*wěi jiǔ*) **and the six kinds of food** (*wěi shí*), **thus cultivating** (*jiàn zuò jiàqǐng*) **the Five Cereals** (*wǔxià*).
**Imitation** (*qiè nǐ*) **of the** (*zhī*) **Five** (*wǔ*) **Five** (*wǔ*).

In ancient times, **tortoiseshell** (*bǎo guī*) **was treasured** (*bǎo*) **and cowrie shells** (*huò bèi*) **were currency** (*bì*).
Later generations of **scholars** (*jūnzǐ*) **exchanged** (*yì*) **them for gold coins** (*jīnbì*), **to facilitate** (*yǐ tōng*) **the state** (*guójiā*) **and rely upon** (*wàn mín yǐ lài*) **the people** (*mín*).
**Imitation** (*qiè nǐ*) **of the** (*zhī*) **thoughts** (*sī*).

All versions read **"thoughts and deliberations"** (*sīlǜ*), but **"deliberations"** (*lǜ*) seems to be a superfluous character.
**Establishing lords and opening kingdoms** (*jiàn hòu kāiguó*), **dissolving titles and ranking officials** (*huàn jié bān zhì*).
**To attract the myriad blessings** (*yǐ yǐn bǎi lù*), **imitation** (*qiè nǐ*) **of the** (*zhī*) **blessing** (*fú*).

**Vexation** (*yuè yǎn*) **without order** (*bù lìng*), **the use of the Five Punishments** (*wéi yòng wǔ xíng*).
**Imitation** (*qiè nǐ*) **of the** (*zhī*) **calamity** (*huò*).

**Holding the jade tablet** (*bǐng guī*), **wearing the jade conch** (*dài bì*), **displaying the ranks of the myriad ministers** (*lù cù qún bì*).
**Lù** pronounced as *lì jū* (力居切), **to array in order** (*chén xù*).
**Imitation** (*qiè nǐ*) **of the** (*zhī*) **Eighty-One** (*bāshí yī*) **Chapters** (*shǒu*).

**Thornwood** (*jí mù*) **as shuttle** (*zhù*), **carved wood** (*xiāo mù*) **as spindle** (*zhóu*).
Once the **shuttle and spindle** (*zhùzhóu*) **were set in place** (*jì shī*), **the people obtained** (*mín dé yǐ*) **warmth** (*yàn*).
**Imitation** (*qiè nǐ*) **of the** (*zhī*) **warp and weft** (*jīngwěi*).

**Carving and cutting** (*diāo gē*) **the gourd** (*páo*), **bamboo** (*zhú*), **leather** (*gé*), **wood** (*mù*), **clay** (*tǔ*), **metal** (*jīn*), **striking stones** (*jī shí*) **and plucking silk** (*dàn sī*).
**To harmonize the world** (*yǐ hé tiānxià*), **imitation** (*qiè nǐ*) **of the** (*zhī*) **Eight Winds** (*bā fēng*).

**Dīng** lacks the **"carving"** (*diāo*) character; other versions have only **"cutting"** (*gē*).
**Zhāng** reads **"engrave"** (*kè*).
**The *Shìwén*** (《释文》) reads **"then"** (*zé*), pronounced as *xuān*.

It says **"carving"** (*diāo*) is **one** (*yī*) **variant of "cutting"** (*gē*), **Sòng** and **Xǔ** read **"carving and cutting"** (*diāo gē*).
**Diāo** pronounced as *diāo*, **likely the same ancient character** (*gǎizì tóng*).

**Yin and Yang interweaving** (*yīn yáng xiāng cuò*), **men and women not crossing paths** (*nánnǚ bù xiāng shè*).
**People and things** (*rén wù*) **each follow their own kind** (*rù jué wéi huì*), **imitation** (*qiè nǐ*) **of the** (*zhī*) **emptiness and abundance** (*xū yíng*).

**Sun and Moon interchanging** (*rì yuè xiāng hú*), **stars and constellations not colliding** (*xīng chén bù xiāng chù*).
**Sounds and rhythms** (*yīn lǜ*) **diverging in order** (*chā liè*), **odd and even** (*jī ǒu*) **contrasting in essence** (*yì qì*).
**Father and son differing in appearance** (*fù zǐ shū miàn*), **brothers not twins** (*xiōng dì bù luán*).
**Luán** pronounced as *shēng huàn* (生患切) and *suǒ juàn* (所眷切), **twins** (*shuāngshēng zǐ*).
**Sòng** reads **"breed"** (*zī*).

**No two emperors alike** (*dì wáng mò tóng*), **imitation** (*qiè nǐ*) **of the** (*zhī*) **year** (*suì*).

Those who gnash with teeth are hornless in youth,
Those who fly are two-footed in their limbs—
Without horns or wings, they are shaped by **virtue/power** (*dé*) and **Way** (*dào*),
**Imitating** (*qiè nǐ*) the **nine days** of equal division.

To preserve what is seen and know what is hidden,
To approximate the near and infer the distant,
To probe the **Dao**’s boundless depths and fathom the **Divine’s** mysteries,
**Imitating** the **shadows and measures** (*guǐ kè*).

One bright, one obscure—
Falling into **rigidity**, falling into **softness**,
Those who know **yin** act in reverse,
Those who know **yang** flow with it—
**Imitating** the **day and night**.

Above and below, both seeking—
Following **Heaven’s** measure;
Past and future, both recounting—
Following **Heaven’s** method;
None dare alter or forge—
Following **Heaven’s** **flaws** (*chǒu*)—
**Imitating** the **Heavenly Principle** (*Tiān Yuán*).

**Heaven and Earth**, divine siblings, conform to the *Yì*’s law—
Endless, unceasing, the past concludes while the future begins,
**Imitating** the **Wú** (罔), **Zhí** (直), **Méng** (蒙), **Qiú** (酋), **Míng** (冥).

Thus, to **imitate** water in the river, water finds its tameness;
To **imitate** conduct in **virtue/power** (*dé*), conduct finds its center;
To **imitate** speech in **law**, speech finds its rectitude.
When speech is rectified, there is no rejection;
When conduct is centered, there is no deviation;
When water flows顺 (*shùn*), there is no ruin.
Without ruin, it endures;
Without deviation, it is observed;
Without rejection, it is heeded.
To be heeded is the **Sage’s** ultimate attainment;
To be observed is the **Sage’s** **virtue/power** (*dé*);
To endure is the **Way** of **Heaven and Earth**.

*(Chapter heading: "Business" [业])*

Thus, in ancient times, when the **Sages** undertook their works,
They **imitated** **Heaven** above, **Earth** below, and **humanity** within.
**Heaven and Earth** formed the **case** (*hán*), **Sun and Moon** fixed their brilliance,
The **Five Phases** encompassed **flaws** (*chǒu*), the **Five Peaks** dominated the mountains,
The **Four Seas** lengthened the rivers, the **Five Classics** grasped the **squares** (*jǔ*).
When **Heaven** rebels, **Earth** rebels, **humanity** rebels,
Then the great affairs of the world are perverted.

The **Mysterious’s** praise-words are all **imitations**.
**Qi** generates **kinds**, **kinds** generate the **hurried** (*jié zú*) of affairs—
Truly, they follow the **Three Models** (*sān mó*).
Observing all the **imitations**’ (*qiè nǐ*) purposes,
One may glimpse the **praise’s** intent,
Though not exhausting their **gatherings** (*huì*), one attains **comparative meaning** (*bǐ yì*).

Reflect with **emptiness** (*xū*), weigh **calamity and blessing** to adapt—
Like **gold coins** circulating through the world.
Assembling all **lords** (*bì*), **imitating** the **eighty-one heads** (*shǒu*),
Then only the **essence** (*tǐ*) remains.
The **Mysterious Ultimate** (*Xuán Jī*) is supreme—
Presiding over this **emptiness and abundance** (*xū yíng*), within a single **day and night**,
Yet the **year’s** cycles are complete, the **Way**’s shifts differing yet never conflicting.
But the **essence** has great and small—
Thus the **imitations** have **Mysterious Chapters** (*Xuán Zhāng*).
The **Mysterious**, with two heads, equally divides the **nine days**—
Profit cannot be monopolized; this is **Heaven’s Way**.

The **Mysterious Classic’s** symbolic words
Truly **imitate** the **shadows and measures** (*guǐ kè*), **day and night**,
And number the **Heavenly Principle** (*Tiān Yuán*).
The **Heavenly Principle** is where the **cycles**, **chapters**, and **statutes** converge.

The *Yì* says:
*"Exhausted, it transforms; transformed, it flows; flowing, it endures."*
**Wú** and **Méng**—truly the **divine siblings**.
Beginning and end, unceasing—
This follows the *Yì* thus.

**The Ninth Chapter of the *Tàixuān Wén*’s *Qiè Nǐ* concludes.**
#1 *"Day"* (*rì*) originally *"Say"* (*yuē*), corrected per the **Fan** edition.
#2 *"Un"* (*wèi*) originally *"End"* (*mò*), corrected per the **Fan** edition.

---
**The Tenth Chapter of the *Tàixuān Tú*’s *Gào* begins.**
**The *Xuán Tú***

**The Third Transformation of the *Xuán Tú***

The **One Primordial** covers the **Three Directions**—
Each **Direction** mirrors the **Nine Provinces**,
Branches bear the **Multitudes of Departments**,
Divisions govern the **Clans of Families**—
All affairs dwell within.

The **Yin Essence** aligns with the **Northern Dipper**,
While **Day and Moon** trace their **boundaries**.
**Yin and Yang** interweave in **hidden exchange**,
The **Four Seasons** lurk in **latent abode**.
The **Five Phases** move in **concealed courses**,
The **Six Extremes** blend in **harmony**,
The **Seven Mansions** pivot on the **axis**.

**Taming the Profound**, the **Nine Nines** manifest—
**Six Jia** internalized, **Lü** and **Yue** in **hidden resonance**.
**Law and Measure** conceal their **cycles**.

*The Diagram’s Image* extols the **Primordial Form**,
Praising the **fulfillment of success**.

**First**, the **Central Excess** follows—
A hundred **plants** sway in **procession**,
Then **heaven is questioned**.
*Question* (*xùn*) is homophonous with *Swift*.
**Thunder** shakes the **procession’s side**,
**Zhen** resounds—*Zhen* pronounced as *Jin*.
*The procession’s side*—Ding’s *yú* reads *yǔ*.

**Yin** praises the **gentle subtlety**,
**Uprooting** from the **Primordial**.
The **East stirs the Azure Dragon**,
Its **light departs from the Abyss**.
**Crushing** all **ten thousand things**,
**Heaven and Earth** renew their **procession**.
*—* The **cut** (*tuī*) is **urgent** and **piercing**.

**Central**, the **Expanded Vision**—
**Heaven’s weight** shines **double-bright**,
**Thunder and Wind** dazzle in **radiance**,
Moving with **all things in season**.
The **Yin Chief** dominates the **West-North**,
The **Yang** lingers in the **East-South**.
Though **internal responses** exist,
**External resistance** meets **rigid constancy**.
The **Dragon** stands firm in **Heaven**,
Its **length** boundless—
**Southward conquest** brings **disaster**,
**Encountering the Shattered Light**.
*Chapter* reads *"Encounter the Shattered Light"* (*yù hū bēng guāng*),
*Sòng* reads *"Encounter at the Shattered Light"* (*yù yú bēng guāng*).

**Final**, the **Diminished Depth**—
**Heaven’s Root** returns **inward**,
**Qi** refines, **essence** condenses.
**Surveying** all **multitudes**,
Each **bows in hardship**.
**Deeply merging** with **Yellow Purity**,
**Broadly containing** all **life**,
The **Great Handle** clouds **in motion**,
**Timely overseeing** the **Earth’s design**.
**Perverse schemes** ascend in **absorption**,
Then **tame the numinous spirits**,
**Encompassing** **beginning and end**—
**Heaven, Earth, and Human** virtues all **rigid and constant**.

This is the **third transformation** of the *Xuán Tú*.
**Directions, Provinces, Departments, Families**—
**One, Two, One-Two, Four**—
While the **Primordial** dwells within—
This is called **"Five merging with the Void."**

**Thunder shakes** #1;
*The procession’s side* is **Lún**—
The **Pheasant’s cry** in **late winter** responds.

**Yin** praises the **gentle subtlety**,
**Uprooting** from the **Primordial**—
The **Great Cluster’s qi**.
The **East stirs the Azure Dragon**,
Its **light departs from the Abyss**—
Then **dissolution** follows.

At the **rigid constancy’s hour**,
The **Dragon** seeks only **proliferation**—
**Conquest** then brings **disaster**.

**Heaven’s Root** returns—
The **One’s reversal**,
From **difficult cultivation**.
**Deeply merging** with **Yellow Purity**—
Then **restored to the Center**.
The **Great Handle** clouds **in motion**,
**Timely overseeing** the **Earth’s design**—
The **Dipper’s revolution** aligns the **Five Celestial Stems**.
**Perverse schemes** ascend in **absorption**,
Then **tame the numinous spirits**—
Thus **praising fulfillment of success**,
**Planning and seizing**—
Nothing remains unattained.

Hence, it **tames the numinous spirits** without **contradiction**,
**Encompasses** **beginning and end**—
All **virtues** are **rigid and constant**.

**Heaven’s field** is its **Way**,
**Earth’s** its **threads**.
*Rú* (*zhì*), pronounced *zhí-zhǐ*.
*The Odes* say:
*"Split the firewood, stack it up"* #2—
Meaning **follow its principle**.

**Yin and Yang** intermingle in **proximity**,
Some **male**, some **female**.
**Heaven’s Way** forms **rules**,
**Earth’s Way** forms **measures**.
**Rules** move in **circular process**,
**Measures** rest in **stability**.
**Circular process** thus attains **numinous clarity**,
**Stability** thus gathers **kindred types**.
**Kindred types** thus **enrich**,
**Numinous clarity** thus **ascends to nobility**.

The **Primordial**—
**Heaven’s Way**, **Earth’s Way**, **Human Way**—
**Combining the Three Ways**, it is named **Heaven**.
The **Way of Sovereign and Minister, Father and Son, Husband and Wife**.
**Extending** the **Way of Sovereign and Minister, Father and Son, Husband and Wife**,
It **unites with Heaven**.

The **Primordial** has **two Ways**:
*Sòng* reads: *"The Primordial with **one Way**,
**Three births**, **one origin**,
**One generating three**."*
**One origin**—
**Directions, Provinces, Departments, Families**.
**One generating three**,
**One originating three**—
**Directions, Provinces, Departments, Families**.
**Three births**—
**Triple-parting the Yang Qi**,
Forming **three layers**, extreme as **nine encampments**.
This is **"same root, divergent ends."**
*Fàn* reads: *"Same root, divergent births."*
*Chapter* reads *"say"* (*yuē*), *birth* (*shēng*).
*Lín* reads *birth* (*shēng*), *same root* (*tóng běn*), *divergent ends* (*lí shēng*).

**The Essence of Heaven and Earth**.
**Laterally communicating** **above and below**—
All **things converge**.
**Nine encampments** flow **circularly**—
**Beginning and end** are **rigid and constant**.
**Beginning** in the **eleventh month**,
**Ending** in the **tenth month**,
**Luo** repeats **nine courses**,
Each **forty days**.

**Sincerity within** resides in the **Center**,
**Propagated outward** resides in the **Excess**,
**Cloud-motion, rain-bestowal** resides in the **Following**,
**Changing nodes, shifting degrees** resides in the **Reversion**,
**Precious light, pure completeness** resides in the **Vision**—
*Pure completeness*—*Chapter* reads *"pure gold"* (*chún jīn*).
**Void within, vast without** resides in the **Expansion**,
**Trimming, retreat, consumption** resides in the **Diminution**,
**Descending, concealing** resides in the **Depth**—
*Queue* (*duì*) pronounced *duì* (as *zhuì*).
**Examining the terminal nature** resides in the **Completion**.

Thus, **One to Nine**—
The **Yin-Yang ebb-and-flow’s calculation**—
Reversed and displayed:
**Child**—**Yang** is born in the **eleventh month**,
**Yin** terminates in the **tenth month**—visible.
**Wu**—**Yin** is born in the **fifth month**,
**Yang** terminates in the **fourth month**—visible.
**Generating Yang** is none greater than **Child**,
**Generating Yin** is none greater than **Wu**.
**West-North**—**Child’s** beauty is **exhausted**,
**East-South**—**Wu’s** beauty is **extreme**.

Thus, **contemplate the Heart at One**,
**Reflect repeatedly at Two**,
**Fulfill intent at Three**,
**Unfurl clarity at Four**,
**Manifest brilliance at Five**,
**Reach grandeur at Six**,
**Decay and loss at Seven**,
**Peeling and falling at Eight**,
**Extinction at Nine**.

**Generating the numinous** is none earlier than **One**,
**Central harmony** is none greater than **Five**,
**Arrogance and excess** are none more constrained than **Nine**.

「**Arrogance (倨)**, pronounced *jù*, means proud.
**Swiftness (勋)**, pronounced *xūn*, means hasty.

Guo Yuanheng’s commentary: **Excess (剧)** is used instead of *勋*.

As for **One (一)**, it is the subtle beginning of contemplation.
**Four (四)** is the foundation of fortune.
**Seven (七)** is the threshold of misfortune.

**Three (三)** is the peak of contemplation,
**Six (六)** is the zenith of fortune,
**Nine (九)** is the exhaustion of misfortune.

**Two (二), Five (五), and Eight (八)** are the midpoints of the three phases—fortune advances, misfortune withdraws.

**Nine (九)** is the void where the **Eight Trigrams (八卦)** are arranged, the **Noble (君子)** and the **Petty (小人)** alike using it as their **palace (宫)**.

From **One (一)** to **Three (三)**, one endures poverty and lowliness while the heart labors.
From **Four (四)** to **Six (六)**, one attains wealth and nobility with honor and height.
From **Seven (七)** to **Nine (九)**, one avoids calamity but falls into ruin.

Below **Five (五)**, one follows the **principle of nurturing (作息)**;
Above **Five (五)**, one follows the **principle of diminishing (作消)**.

When the count is high, one sees nobility but is truly depleted;
When the count is low, one sees lowliness but is truly abundant.

All (作) is either **void and excess (虚饶)** or **substance and excess (实饶)**—
**Nurturing (息)** and **diminishing (消)** are intertwined,
Nobility (贵) and lowliness (贱) are exchanged.

Fortune arrives while misfortune departs;
Misfortune arrives while fortune flees.

**Xu (许)** and **Huang (黄)** omit the line *"Fortune arrives..."*.
**Song (宋)** and **Ding (丁)** place *"Misfortune arrives..."* above.

Here, we follow the **Zhou (章)** text.

The **Dao/Way (道)** is profound yet lowly, extreme yet elevated.
**Day (昼)** and **night (夜)** alternate—**marriage (夫妇)** is their bond.
**End and beginning (终始)** generate each other—**parent and child (父子)** perpetuate this.
**Sun and Moon (日月)** unite and separate—**ruler and minister (君臣)** fulfill their duty.
**First and last (孟季)** follow order—**senior and junior (长幼)** observe their boundaries.
**Pairs (两两)** complement each other—**friends (朋友)** gather thus.

One **day (日)** is made of one **daytime (昼)** and one **nighttime (夜)**.
One **Yin (阴)** and one **Yang (阳)** generate all **ten thousand things (万物)**.

When daytime counts are high and nighttime counts are low,
The **Zhou (章)** text also notes extended day and shortened night—**divergence (衍)**.

**Song (宋)** states: *"Daytime counts are high, nighttime counts are low."*
**Symbol (象)** observes the Moon’s waxing and the Sun’s waning.

When the **Noble (君子)** acts with radiance and the **Petty (小人)** acts in obscurity,
The **Dao/Way (道)** of the **Noble (君子)** is complete,
While the **Dao/Way (道)** of the **Petty (小人)** is lacking.

To **begin (始)** with the **Three (三)** is structured—**position (位)** is thus established.
To **generate (生)** with the **Three (三)** is boundless—**Qi (气)** thus creates and transforms.

The **Three (三)** divide **Yang Qi (阳气)** into **beginning (始), middle (中), and end (终)**.
The **Nine Heavens (九天)** revolve in cycles—
**Beginning (始)** at the **first day of the eleventh month (十一月朔旦)**, the **Winter Solstice (冬至)**,
While the **middle (中)** aligns with it.

After **forty-five days (四十日半)**, the **Great Cold (大寒)**, then **Xian (羡)** aligns with it.
Again after **forty-five days (四十日半)**, **Awakening of Insects (惊蛰)**, then **Cong (从)** aligns with it.
Then **Grain Rain (谷雨)**, **Xiao (賥)** aligns with it;
**Lesser Fullness (小满)**, **Kuo (廓)** aligns with it;
**Lesser Heat (小暑)**, **Jian (减)** aligns with it;
**Dewey Heat (处暑)**, **Chen (沈)** aligns with it;
**Autumnal Equinox (秋分)**, **Cheng (成)** aligns with it;
**Established Winter (立冬)**, completing the **Qi (气)** of the cycle.

The **Nine Heavens (九天)** total **three hundred sixty-four and a half days (日)**, and thus the year is fulfilled.

When the **day (日)** advances **forty-five days (四十日)**, its halves diverge—**this is how Heaven’s revolutions (运)** occur.

**Three (三)** are divided into **four (四)**, reaching **eighty-one (八十一)**;
**Nine (九)** are arranged in **three (三) and six (六)**, reaching **seven hundred twenty-nine (七百二十九)**.

Thus, from **beginning (始), middle (中), and end (终)**,
To **contemplate (思), fortune (福), and misfortune (祸)**,
To exhaust the **calculations of Yin and Yang (阴阳消息之计)**.

**Profound (玄)** encompasses **three hundred sixty-four nights (夜)** and **three hundred sixty-five days (昼)**,
This is **daytime counts high, nighttime counts low—Yang in excess, Yin in depletion (阳饶而阴乏)**.

**One (一)** and **Six (六)** share the same **root (宗)**;
**Two (二)** and **Seven (七)** are **companions (朋)**;
**Three (三)** and **Eight (八)** form **harmony (友)**;
**Four (四)** and **Nine (九)** follow the same **Dao/Way (道)**;
**Five (五)** guards itself with **Five (五)**.

**Profound (玄)** has **one ruler (规), one measure (矩), one cord (绳), one standard (准)**,
To conform to the **crossing Dao/Way (横天地之道)**,
To tame the **numbers of Yin and Yang (阴阳之数)**,
To emulate their **numinous brilliance (神明)**,
To illuminate their **profound darkness (幽昏)**.

Then the **Dao/Way (道)** of the **eight directions (八方)** can be discerned.

**Three (三)** and **Eight (八)** form the **ruler (规)**;
**Four (四)** and **Nine (九)** form the **measure (矩)**;
**Two (二)** and **Seven (七)** form the **cord (绳)**;
**One (一)** and **Six (六)** form the **standard (准)**.

With **boundaries (界)** distinguished and **corners (辨)** divided,
The **Dao/Way (道)** of the **eight directions (八方)** can be discerned.

**Profound (玄)** has the **number of Six Nine (六九)**,
**Strategy (策)** uses **Three Six (三六)**,
**Ceremony (仪)** uses **Two Nine (二九)**.
**Profound (玄)** employs **eighteen (十有八)** in its calculations!

The **essence of Tai (泰积)** begins with **eighteen strategies (十有八策)**,
Ends with **fifty-four (五十有四)**.

Combining the **beginning (始)** and **end (终)** strategies,
Half of it is **Tai’s center (泰中)**.

The **strategies of Tai’s center (泰中)** are **thirty-six (三十有六)**,
Used to govern **seven hundred twenty-nine (七百二十九)**,
Totaling **twenty-six thousand two hundred forty-four strategies (策)** for the **Tai cycle (泰积)**.

**Seventy-two strategies (策)** make one day,
Totaling **three hundred sixty-four and a half days (日)**,
Filling the **year (岁)** and aligning with its **days (日)** while governing the **calendar (历)**.

Thus, from **Child (子)** to **Chen (辰)**,
From **Chen (辰)** to **Shen (申)**,
From **Shen (申)** to **Child (子)**, crowned with **Jia (甲)**,
And **Zhou (章), Hui (会), Tong (统), Yuan (元)** all vanish together with **eclipses (月食)**—this is the **Profound Dao/Way (玄之道)**.

**Ding (丁)** and **Song (宋)** state: *"Vanish with eclipses (月食没), the fullness of the **Profound Dao/Way (玄道)**."*
**Zhou (章)** states: *"Vanish with **moon’s occultation (月蚀)**—this is the fullness of the **Profound Dao/Way (玄之道)**."*

Heaven uses **Six (六)** as **nodes (节)**—**Yin within Yang (阳中之阴)**.
Earth uses **Nine (九)** to **govern gatherings (制会)**—**Yang within Yin (阴中之阳)**.
**Yin and Yang (阴阳)** transform and interact—**thus utility and life (利用生)** arise.

**Strategy (策)** mirrors **Heaven’s numbers (天数)**,
Earth **conforms (仪)** to Heaven and **matches (匹)** it,
Humans **observe the law (法)** therein.

Thus, its numbers begin with **eighteen strategies (十有八策)**,
End with **fifty-four (五十有四)**.

The **numbers of Heaven, Earth, and Humans (天地人数)**,
**Begin and end (始终)** in alignment,
And **Profound (玄)** takes **eighteen strategies (十有八)** as its **root (宗)**.

Thus, combining **fifty-four (五十有四)** to make **seventy-two (七十有二)**,
This is the **strategy (策)** of one **day (日)** and one **night (夜)**.

And one **year (岁)** mirrors this,
So **seven hundred twenty-nine (七百二十九)** are governed by **Tai’s center (泰中)** at **thirty-six (三十有六)**.

Each **cycle (赞)** has **thirty-six strategies (策)**,
Accumulating to **twenty-six thousand two hundred forty-four strategies (策)** to complete the year.

**Zhou (章), Xian (羡), Cong (从)** from **Child (子)** to **Chen (辰)**,
**Geng (更), Meng (睟), Kuo (廓)** from **Chen (辰)** to **Shen (申)**,
**Jian (减), Chen (沈), Cheng (成)** from **Shen (申)** to **Child (子)**—
These are the **four phases (方)** of one year.

And **four thousand six hundred seventeen years (岁)** mirror this pattern.

**Nineteen years (十九岁)** form one **Zhou (章)**,
**Twenty-seven chapters (二十七章)** form one **Hui (会)**,
**Three gatherings (三会)** form one **Tong (统)**,
**Three cycles (三统)** form one **Yuan (元)**.

**Tong (统)** totals **one thousand five hundred thirty-nine years (岁)**,
**Jiazi (甲子)** on the **first day of the Winter Solstice (朔旦冬至)** as **Heaven’s cycle (天统)**,
**Jiachen (甲辰)** on the **first day of the Winter Solstice (朔旦冬至)** as **Earth’s cycle (地统)**,
**Jia Shen (甲申)** on the **first day of the Winter Solstice (朔旦冬至)** as **Human’s cycle (人统)**—
Mirroring the **Profound (玄)**’s **three phases (三方)**.

When eclipses vanish together with the moon, the **Tong (统)** encompasses **eighty-one chapters (章)**, the **Yuan (元)** encompasses **nine gatherings (会)**, and each gathering exhausts the count of lunar eclipses.

Lunar eclipses are the **fullness of numbers (数之盈)**.
Lu Ji (陆绩) said: *"Divide the total of one **Yuan (元)** by nine gatherings, and it will be fully exhausted."*

When the **intercalary division (闰分)** of one **chapter (章)** is complete, when the lunar eclipses of one **gathering (会)** are exhausted, when the **new moon divisions (朔分)** of one **Tong (统)** are complete, and when the **six Jia (六甲)** of one **Yuan (元)** are fulfilled—

The **Profound (玄)** reveals:
The **Profound (玄)** generates **two divine forms (神象二)**,
The **two divine forms** generate **the standard (规)**,
The **standard** generates **three models (三摹)**,
The **three models** generate **nine foundations (九据)**.

The **Profound (玄)** refines once and attains **Heaven (天)**, hence it is called **Nine Heavens (九天)**.
*(Later editions read "nine" instead of "have." Earth and Human follow the same.)*
Refined twice, it attains **Earth (地)**, hence it is called **Nine Earths (九地)**.
Refined thrice, it attains **Human (人)**, hence it is called **Nine Humans (九人)**.

Heaven completes in **three foundations (三据)**, hence it is called **Beginning, Middle, End (始、中、终)**.
Earth takes form in **three foundations**, hence it is called **Below, Middle, Above (下、中、上)**.
Human manifests in **three foundations**, hence it is called **Thought, Fortune, Calamity (思、福、祸)**.

*"Below inhales, above exhales"*—**hūhéqiè (呼合切)**, as in *"yìn (歠)"* in the *Shuōwén (说文)*.
It traverses the **Nine Voids (九虚)**;
Through **small and great threads (小索大索)**, it revolves **nine degrees (九度)**.

The **Profound (玄)** is the **leader of the divine (神之魁)**.
Heaven’s **Profound (玄)** is unseen,
Earth’s **Profound (玄)** is formless,
Human’s **Profound (玄)** is the **heart and abdomen**.

Heaven’s **mystic orifice (奥)** is the **west-north (西北)**, where **dense transformations refine essence (郁化精)**.
Earth’s **mystic orifice** is **Huángquán (黄泉)**—*(later editions read "Huángyuān (黄渊)")*—
This is the **hidden soul and glory (隐魄荣)**.
Human’s **mystic orifice** is **thought and deliberation (思虑)**, containing the **ultimate essence (至精)**.
*(Later editions read "合 (harmony)" instead of "含 (contain)")*.

Heaven’s **vault (穹)** is arched and encircles below,
Earth’s **flanks (旁薄)** lean upward,
Human **dwells (处)** in between.
*(Later editions read "苠 (jì)" instead of the obscured character.)*

Heaven is **pure and unrestrained (浑)**, hence its motion is ceaseless.
Earth is **decayed and still (颓而静)**, hence its generation is not delayed.
Human is **tamed by Heaven and Earth (驯乎天地)**, hence its actions are inexhaustible.

Heaven and Earth oppose each other,
The sun and moon **intersect (相刿)**,
Mountains and rivers **flow toward each other (相流)**,
Light and heavy **float in balance (相浮)**,
Yin and yang **weave (相绩)**,
Superior and inferior **do not transgress (不相黩)**.

Thus, Earth is **hollowed (坎)** while Heaven is **stern (严)**,
The moon **hurries (遄)** while the sun **lingers (湛)**.

The **Five Phases** alternately reign,
The **Four Seasons** never peak together.
The sun **shines brightly (昱)** in the day,
The moon **shines brightly (昱)** in the night;
**Mǎo (昴)** ascends in winter,
**Fire** ascends in summer.

South and north **fix their positions (定位)**,
East and west **communicate qi (通气)**,
All things **intertwine within (错离)**.

The **Profound (玄)** manifests **one virtue (一德)** and generates **Five Births (五生)**,
It manifests **one punishment (一刑)** and generates **Five Subductions (五克)**.
*(Later editions include "玄" before "一刑.")*

The **Five Births** do not **exhaust each other (不相殄)**,
The **Five Subductions** do not **contradict each other (不相逆)**.
Not exhausting allows **succession (相继)**,
Not contradicting allows **governance (相治)**.
Succession is the **Way of parent and child (父子之道)**,
Governance is the **treasure of ruler and subject (君臣之宝)**.

From the **Profound Darkness (玄冥)**, **divine light (神光)** emerges,
Hence the **two divine forms (神象二)**.
The **two movements (二运)** are boundless,
Thus the **standard (规)** is generated.
The **standard** is **modeled threefold (三摹)**,
And **Heaven’s Profound (天玄)**, **Earth’s Profound (地玄)**, and **Human’s Profound (人玄)** are attained.

A **model (摹)** must have **foundations (据)** to establish itself,
Hence the **nine foundations (九据)** extend to **seven hundred twenty-nine (七百二十有九)**.

The **nine praises (九赞)** are the **three ultimate Ways (三极之道)**.

Heaven’s **mystic orifice (奥)** in the west-north
Refines **hidden essence (化精)** in the **chaotic void (混沌无端)**.
Earth’s **mystic orifice** in **Huángquán (黄泉)**
Ensures **nothing is absent within (信无不在乎中)**,
Where **all things’ refined qi (精气)** hides.
This is the **hidden soul and glory (魄荣)**, the **time of obscurity (罔之时)**.

What is called **"conceal Heaven to become Heaven (潜天而天)"**,
**"conceal Earth to become Earth (潜地而地)"**—
This is the **ultimate of these orifices (极此奥)**.

The **Profound (玄)** is thus manifested,
Yet humans seek to **craft it (造之)**.
If not abandoning **material things (遗物)** and **separating from humanity (离人)**,
And if **refined thought (精思)** does not **transcend (超诣)**,
Then none can enter.

**Suǒ (摛)** said:
*"To defy is impossible, silence attains its essence (默则得其所)."*
This is the **Profound essence (玄要)**.

When the **Profound (玄)** is attained, **divine clarity (神明)** generates it,
Then **all changes of motion and stillness (动静之变)** are **Profound affairs (玄事)**;
**Rest and calamity, beauty and ugliness (休咎好丑)** are all **Profound laws (玄法)**.

When Heaven and Earth **open and close (阖辟)**,
All things **arise together (并兴)**,
Yet the **Profound remains unmoved (玄不动)**.
If **carved and etched (若雕若刻)**,
**Generations transform endlessly (生生化化)**,
Yet the **Profound does nothing (玄无为)**.
To **analyze desires and guide wisdom (析愿迪哲)**,
To **command deceit and destroy depravity (诏奸陨慝)**,
To **organize all measures (百度厘举)**—
Yet the **Profound does not resist (玄莫违)**.

From **beginning to end (始终)**, they **intertwine (相纠)**,
From **ancient to present (古今)**, they **oscillate (相荡)**,
The **Tong and Yuan are endless (统元无尽)**,
Yet the **Profound does not pass (玄不逝)**.

Is this not what is said:
*"All things are complete within me,
The Dao-heart is only subtle (道心惟微)?"*

The **Non-dual (不二)** is the **constant of the Profound (玄之常)**;
The **dual (凡二)** is the **variation of the divine (神之变)**.

The **Profound** records the **"Book of the Dipper (斗书)"**—*(later editions read "Profound Dipper Book (玄日斗书)")*—
Yet the moon is not recorded,
Always **full (常满)**, to **counter the void (以御虚)**.
*(Later editions include "日 (sun)" before "常满.")*

When a year is **complete and serene (宁悉)**, the **season is diseased (年病)**.
In **nineteen years (十九年)**, there are **seven intercalations (七闰)**—
This is **Heaven’s compensation (天之偿)**.

Yang **moves and exhales (动吐)**,
Yin **stills and inhales (静翕)**;
The **Way of Yang is always abundant (阳道常饶)**,
The **Way of Yin is always deficient (阴道常乏)**—
This is the **Way of Yin and Yang (阴阳之道)**.
*(Later editions read "阳动而吐，阴静而翕.")*

When Heaven is **strong and healthy (强健)**, it **soars high (侨躆)**—
*"Sōu (侨)"* is pronounced *"qú xiāo (渠消)"* (high),
Or it may be read as *"luó (蹻)"* (reside outside), *"jū biǎo (居表)"*.
*"Dù (躆)"* is pronounced *"jù (据)"*.

A day and night **self-renew with surplus (自复而有余)**.
The sun has **south and north (南有北)**,
The moon has **forward and return (往有来)**.
If the sun **neither goes south nor north (不南不北)**,
Then there is **no winter nor summer (无冬无夏)**;
If the moon **neither goes forward nor returns (不往不来)**,
Then the **full and new moons do not form (望晦不成)**.

The **Sage observes** the **variations of hidden and revealed (脁朒侧匿)**—
*"Zhuì (脁)"* is pronounced *"chù liǎo (敕了)"*.
*(Later editions omit "朒," reading only "脁.")*
And **regulates the sequence of solar and lunar gender (日月雌雄之序)**,
Establishing it **without end (经之於无已)**.

Thus, the **Profound** **weaves the celestial threads (鸿纶天元)**,
**Binding (娄)** and **restraining (钳)** what is to come—
*(Later editions read "拙将来者乎" instead of "钳之.")*
*"Hù (乎)"* may also be read as *"yě (也)"*.

**Three hundred sixty-five degrees and a quarter (三百六十五度四分度之一)**
Complete the **circuit of Heaven (周乎天)**.
A year of **twelve months** advances **three hundred fifty-four degrees and a tenth (凡行三百五十四度而十度四分度之一)**
And enters the **following year (入於嗣岁)**.

「The so-called *intercalary month* (**閏**, *rùn*) is the accumulation of this *oddity* (**奇**, *qí*).

When the movement does not reach the **full measure of Heaven’s degrees** (**天度**, *tiāndù*), then this year is **deficient** (**病**, *bìng*).
Therefore, an **intercalary month** is added to compensate for it.
In **nineteen years**, seven **intercalary months** (**七閏**, *qī rùn*) are applied,
And thus the **year is made complete** (**岁宁悉**, *suì níngxī*).

The **Profound Dao** (**玄经**, *Xuánjīng*) mirrors the **year’s progression** (**岁**, *suì*), hence it is said:
*"Eighty-one chapters"* (**八十一首**, *bāshíyī shǒu*), and all **matters of the year are perfected** (**岁事咸贞**, *suìshì xiánzhēng*).
When **completeness is without deficiency** (**宁无不安**, *níng wú bù’ān*) and **perfection is without excess** (**悉无不足**, *xī wú bùzú*), this is the **fulfillment of the canon** (**章之成**, *zhāng zhī chéng*).

*"Zhuì"* (**脁**, *zhuì*) refers to the **Moon’s swift movement** (**月行疾**, *yuè xíngjí*);
*"Nǎi"* (**朒**, *nǎi*) refers to the **Moon’s slow movement** (**月行迟**, *yuè xíngchí*).
When the **waning phase is visible in the west**, it is called *"Zhuì"* (**晦见于西谓之脁**, *huì jiàn yú xī wèi zhī zhuì*);
When the **new moon is visible in the east**, it is called *"Nǎi"* (**朔见于东谓之朒**, *shuò jiàn yú dōng wèi zhī nǎi*).

*"Sè"* (**侧**, *sè*) and *"Nì"* (**匿**, *nì*) refer to **deviations from its proper course** (**失正行**, *shī zhèngxíng*).
When **the Great is without bounds** (**大无方**, *Dà wúfāng*) and **the Easy is without fixed times** (**易无时**, *Yì wúshí*), then **it becomes the realm of spirits and ghosts** (**神鬼**, *shén guǐ*).
*(Later editions read "大无方无时，然后为鬼神" instead of "大无方，易无时，然后为神鬼也," omitting the "也" and treating "神鬼" as "鬼神.")*

The **Divine** **concludes at the Six Canons** (**神终乎六宗**, *shén zhōng hū liù zōng*).
*(Later editions: "游" [yóu] for "宗"; "斿" [zhuì] in Huang’s text—likely an ancient variant.)*
**The vital essence animates all things** (**魂魂万物**, *hún hún wànwù*), ever **moving and surging** (**动而常冲**, *dòng ér cháng chōng*).

Thus, the **Profound Dao’s discourse** (**玄之辞**, *Xuán zhī cí*) is:
**Deep** to **plumb the depths** (**沉以穷乎下**, *chén yǐ qióng hū xià*);
**Light** to **reach the heights** (**浮以际乎上**, *fú yǐ jì hū shàng*);
**Curve** to **attain straightness** (**曲而端**, *qū ér duān*);
**Scatter** yet **to gather** (**散而聚**, *sàn ér jù*).
Its **greatness** is not **fully tasted** (**美也不尽於味**, *měi yě bù jìn yú wèi*);
Its **magnitude** is not **exhausted in its expanse** (**大也不尽其汇**, *dà yě bù jìn qí huì*).

**Above and below are interconnected** (**上连下连**, *shàng lián xià lián*), yet **not confined to one direction** (**非一方也**, *fēi yī fāng yě*).
**Near and far have no fixed measure** (**远近无常**, *yuǎn jìn wú cháng*), proceeding **according to kind** (**以类行也**, *yǐ lèi xíng yě*).
Sometimes **abundant**, sometimes **sparse** (**或多或寡**, *huò duō huò guǎ*), yet all **affairs are adapted to clarity** (**事适乎明也**, *shì shì hū míng yě*).

Thus, those who speak well of **Heaven and Earth** use **human affairs** (**善言天地者以人事**, *shàn yán tiāndì zhě yǐ rénshì*);
Those who speak well of **human affairs** use **Heaven and Earth** (**善言人事以天地**, *shàn yán rénshì yǐ tiāndì*).

**Full and new moons** **alternate in succession** (**明晦相推**, *mínghuì xiāng tuī*), while **Sun and Moon** **progress beyond measure** (**而日月逾迈**, *ér rìyuè yú mài*).
**Year after year** **swells in resonance** (**岁岁相荡**, *suìsuì xiāng dàng*), and **Heaven and Earth** **are ever more nurtured** (**而天地弥陶**, *ér tiāndì mí táo*).

This is what is meant by **the Divine and the Bright are inexhaustible** (**之谓神明不穷**, *zhī wèi shén míng bù qióng*).
The **root origin** is **difficult to follow** (**原本者难由**, *yuánběn zhě nányóu*);
The **later branches** are **easy to conform to** (**流末者易从**, *liú mò zhě yì cóng*).

Thus, those who uphold the **Six Canons** are praised for **filial piety** (**有宗祖者则称乎孝**, *yǒu zōngzǔ zhě zé chēng hū xiào*);
Those who order **sovereign and minister** are praised for **loyalty** (**序君臣者则称乎忠**, *xù junchén zhě zé chēng hū zhōng*).
This is the **true proclamation of the Great Instruction** (**实告大训**, *shí gào dà xùn*).

The **Profound Dao’s discourse** is **to exhaust the Divine** (**玄之辞以尽神而已**, *Xuán zhī cí yǐ jìn shén ér yǐ*).
The **Divine generates loyalty and filial piety** (**玄神生忠孝**, *Xuán shén shēng zhōngxiào*);
**Loyalty and filial piety generate benevolence and righteousness** (**忠孝生仁义**, *zhōngxiào shēng rén yì*).

Who would not **practice benevolence** (**孰不为仁**, *shú bù wéi rén*)?
Who would not **embrace righteousness** (**孰不为义**, *shú bù wéi yì*)?

「Thus, its foundation is such that it can remain undiluted. When the **Dao of day and night** (*zhòuyè zhī dào*) is unclear, the affairs of **the Junzi** (*君子*) and **the petty person** (*小人*) become intertwined, then those called **benevolent** (*rén*) may fail to distinguish three times out of ten, and those called **righteous** (*yì*) may enter into what is not righteous without discernment. This would cause conduct to lose its **pure virtue** (*chún dé*), which is not the **true order of Heaven’s command** (*tiān mìng zhī zhèng*).

The **Profound Dao** (*Xuán*) proclaims the **Great Instruction** (*dà xùn*), and thus **correctness prevails** (*zhèng shèng yǐ*).

The **Eleven Chapters** (*Yòu shíyī piān*) are elucidated with the *Exegesis* (*Shìwén*), sourced from Xu Han’s *Phonetic Examination* (*Yīnkǎo*). The **Wang** refers to **Tang Wang Yi** (*王即唐王涯*); the **Chen** refers to **modern Chen Jian** (*陈即近世陈渐*), who compiled *The Performance of the Profound* (*Yǎn Xuán*); the **Wu** refers to **Wu Bi** (*吴秘*), who authored *Phonetic Meanings* (*Yīnyì*); the **Guo** refers to **Guo Yuanheng** (*郭元亨*), who composed *Commentary* (*Shū*); the **Ding** refers to **Ding Wei** (*丁谓*), the **Xu** to **Xu Ang** (*许昂*), the **Zhang** to **Zhang Cha** (*章察*), the **Huang** to **Huang Boshi** (*黄伯思*), and the **Lin** to **Lin Yu**’s edition (*林瑀本*), as stated.

The **Great Profound** (*Tài Xuán*) aligns with the **Han Calendar** (*Hàn lì*). In the **Tài Chū Upper Yuan** (*Tài Chū Shàng Yuán*), the **first month of the first year (Jiazi)** (*正月甲子*), on the **new moon and winter solstice** (*shuò dàn dōng zhì*), there is no excess fraction. After **1,539 years** (*hòu qiān wǔ bǎi sān shí jiǔ suì*), in the year **Jiachen** (*甲辰*), the new moon and winter solstice again align without excess. Another **1,539 years** (*yòu qiān wǔ bǎi sān shí jiǔ suì*) returns to the **Jiazi** alignment, without excess.

**Nineteen years** (*shí jiǔ suì*) constitute **one chapter** (*yī zhāng*), and **twenty-seven chapters** (*èr shí qī zhāng*) amount to **513 years** (*wǔ bǎi yī shí sān suì*), forming **one cycle** (*yī huì*). A **cycle** (*huì*) is the completion of the **interaction of sun and moon** (*rìyuè jiāohuì*).

**Eighty-one chapters** (*bā shí yī zhāng*)—**1,539 years** (*qiān wǔ bǎi sān shí jiǔ suì*)—form **one grand cycle** (*yī tǒng*). From **Zi** (*子*) to **Chen** (*辰*), from **Chen** (*辰*) to **Shen** (*申*), and from **Shen** (*申*) back to **Zi** (*子*), these **four grand cycles** (*fàn sì yīuàn*) span **4,617 years** (*wǔ bǎi liù shí yī qiān suì*).

Each **grand cycle** (*tǒng*) contains **three cycles** (*sān huì*), each **cycle** (*huì*) comprises **twenty-seven chapters** (*èr shí qī zhāng*), and **nine cycles** (*jiǔ huì*) complete **one grand cycle** (*yī yuàn*). Within this, **one chapter** exhausts its **intercalary fraction** (*rùn fèn*), **one cycle** completes its **eclipses** (*yuè shí*), **one grand cycle** fulfills its **new moon divisions** (*shuò fèn*), and **one grand cycle** aligns the **six celestial stems** (*liù jiǎ*) and **ten heavenly branches** (*shí zhī*).

The **Han Calendar** (*Hàn lì*) uses **81** as the **day-law** (*rì fǎ*), with **365 days** (*sān bǎi liù shí wǔ rì*) per year. Multiplying the **day-law** (*rì fǎ*) yields **29,565 fractions** (*èr wàn jiǔ qiān wǔ bǎi liù shí wǔ fèn*), adding **one-fourth of a day** (*yì sì fèn rì zhī yī*), resulting in **20 fractions short** (*èr shí fèn shǎo*), totaling **29,585 fractions short** (*hé èr wàn jiǔ qiān wǔ bǎi bā shí wǔ fèn shǎo*). Dividing by the **twenty-four solar terms** (*èr shí sì qì*), each term receives **1,232 fractions** (*yī qiàn èr bǎi sān shí èr fèn*), with **17 fractions short** (*yú shí qī fèn shǎo*) remaining.

Multiplying by **32** (*sān shí èr*) and **8** (*bā*), the common denominator yields **552** (*wǔ bǎi liù shí èr*). Further division yields **23 seconds** (*èr shí sān miǎo*). Thus, each **solar term** (*qì*) contains **1,232 fractions and 23 seconds** (*yī qiàn èr bǎi sān shí èr fèn èr shí sān miǎo*).

Using **32** (*sān shí èr*) as the **second-mother** (*miǎo mǔ*), each **verse** (*shǒu*) receives **364 fractions and 16 seconds** (*sān bǎi liù shí sì fèn shí liù miǎo*), and each **ode** (*zàn*) receives **40 fractions and 16 seconds** (*sì shí fèn shí liù miǎo*).

To determine the **solar term** (*qì*) in which an **ode** (*zàn*) falls: place the **winter solstice** (*dōng zhì*) **solar term**’s fractions and seconds, then subtract the fractions and seconds of the **verse** (*shǒu*). If the remainder is less than the **verse** (*shǒu*), subtract the fractions and seconds of the **ode** (*zàn*). The remaining fractions and seconds, when calculated, yield **Lesser Cold** (*xiǎo hán*).

For the next **solar term** (*qì*), place the remaining fractions and seconds of the previous term, add the fractions and seconds of the current term, and seek as before. The **star positions** (*xīng*) are as follows:

- **Jiao** (*角*) at **12 degrees** (*shí èr dù*), **Kang** (*亢*) at **9**, **She** (*氏*) at **15**, **Fang** (*房*) at **5**, **Xin** (*心*) at **5**, **Wei** (*尾*) at **18**, **Ji** (*箕*) at **11**—**East** (*dōng*) at **75 degrees** (*qī shí wǔ dù*).
- **Dou** (*斗*) at **26 degrees** (*èr shí liù dù*), **Niu** (*牛*) at **8**, **Nǚ** (*女*) at **12**, **Xu** (*虚*) at **10**, **Wei** (*危*) at **17**, **Shì** (*室*) at **16**, **Bì** (*壁*) at **9**—**North** (*běi*) at **98 degrees** (*jiǔ shí bā dù*).
- **Kuí** (*奎*) at **16 degrees** (*shí liù dù*), **Lǚ** (*娄*) at **12**, **Zhuì** (*冑*) at **14**, **Mǎo** (*昴*) at **11**, **Bì** (*毕*) at **16**, **Zī** (*觜*) at **2**, **Shēn** (*参*) at **9**—**West** (*xī*) at **80 degrees** (*bā shí dù*).
- **Jǐng** (*井*) at **3 + 3 degrees** (*sān + sān dù*), **Guǐ** (*鬼*) at **4**, **Liǔ** (*柳*) at **15**, **Xīng** (*星*) at **7**, **Zhāng** (*张*) at **18**, **Yì** (*翼*) at **18**, **Zhěn** (*轸*) at **17**—**South** (*nán*) at **112 degrees** (*bǎi yī shí èr dù*).

**Quánwěi** (*鹑尾*):
- **Initial** (*chū*) at **Zhang** (*张*) **16 degrees** (*shí liù dù*), marking **Establishing Autumn** (*lì qiū*); **Middle** (*zhōng*) at **Yì** (*翼*) **15 degrees** (*shí wǔ dù*), marking **Processing Heat** (*chǔ shǔ*).

**Shòuxīng** (*寿星*):
- **Initial** (*chū*) at **Zhěn** (*轸*) **12 degrees** (*shí èr dù*), marking **White Dew** (*bái lù*); **Middle** (*zhōng*) at **Jiao** (*角*) **10 degrees** (*shí dù*), marking **Autumnal Equinox** (*qiū fèn*).

**Dàhuǒ** (*大火*):
- **Initial** (*chū*) at **She** (*氏*) **5 degrees** (*wǔ dù*), marking **Cold Dew** (*hán lù*); **Middle** (*zhōng*) at **Fang** (*房*) **5 degrees** (*wǔ dù*), marking **Frost’s Descent** (*shuāng jiàng*).

**Xīmù** (*析木*):
- **Initial** (*chū*) at **Wei** (*尾*) **10 degrees** (*shí dù*), marking **Establishing Winter** (*lì dōng*); **Middle** (*zhōng*) at **Ji** (*箕*) **7 degrees** (*qī dù*), marking **Lesser Snow** (*xiǎo xuě*).

**Dàliáng** (*大梁*):
- **Initial** (*chū*) at **Wèi** (*胃*) **7 degrees** (*qī dù*), marking **Grain Rain** (*gǔ yǔ*) and **Today’s Clear Brightness** (*jīn rì qīng míng*); **Middle** (*zhōng*) at **Mǎo** (*昴*) **8 degrees** (*bā dù*), marking **Clear Brightness** (*qīng míng*) and **Today’s Grain Rain** (*jīn rì gǔ yǔ*).

**Shíshěn** (*实沈*):
- **Initial** (*chū*) at **Bì** (*毕*) **12 degrees** (*shí èr dù*), marking **Establishing Summer** (*lì xià*); **Middle** (*zhōng*) at **Jǐng** (*井*) **initial** (*chū*), marking **Lesser Fullness** (*xiǎo mǎn*).

**Quánshǒu** (*鹑首*):
- **Initial** (*chū*) at **Jǐng** (*井*) **16 degrees** (*shí liù dù*), marking **Grain in Ear** (*máng zhòng*); **Middle** (*zhōng*) at **Jǐng** (*井*) **31 degrees** (*sān shí yī dù*), marking **Summer Solstice** (*xià zhì*).

**Quánhuǒ** (*鹑火*):
- **Initial** (*chū*) at **Liǔ** (*柳*) **9 degrees** (*jiǔ dù*), marking **Lesser Heat** (*xiǎo shǔ*); **Middle** (*zhōng*) at **Zhāng** (*张*) **3 degrees** (*sān dù*), marking **Greater Heat** (*dà shǔ*).

**Xīngjì** (*星纪*):
- **Initial** (*chū*) at **Dou** (*斗*) **12 degrees** (*shí èr dù*), marking **Greater Snow** (*dà xuě*); **Middle** (*zhōng*) at **Qiánniú** (*牵牛*) **initial** (*chū*), marking **Winter Solstice** (*dōng zhì*).

**Xuángāo** (*玄枵*):
- **Initial** (*chū*) at **Wěinǚ** (*婺女*) **8 degrees** (*bā dù*), marking **Lesser Cold** (*xiǎo hán*); **Middle** (*zhōng*) at **Wei** (*危*) **initial** (*chū*), marking **Greater Cold** (*dà hán*).

**Péngzǐ** (*娵訾*):
- **Initial** (*chū*) at **Wei** (*危*) **16 degrees** (*shí liù dù*), marking **Establishing Spring** (*lì chūn*); **Middle** (*zhōng*) at **Yíngshì** (*营室*) **14 degrees** (*shí sì dù*), marking **Awakening of Insects** (*jīng zhè*) and **Today’s Rain Water** (*jīn rì yǔ shuǐ*).

**Jiànglǚ** (*降娄*):
- **Initial** (*chū*) at **Kuí** (*奎*) **5 degrees** (*wǔ dù*), marking **Rain Water** (*yǔ shuǐ*) and **Today’s Awakening of Insects** (*jīn rì jīng zhè*); **Middle** (*zhōng*) at **Lǚ** (*娄*) **Western degree** (*xī dù*), marking **Spring Equinox** (*chūn fèn*).

The **seconds** (*miǎo shù*) being short, the **fractions** (*fèn*) are dispersed into **32** (*sān shí èr*).

To seek the **star** (*xīng*): place its **host degree** (*sù dù shù*), double it with the **verse** (*shǒu*), and subtract the remainder to find the **ode’s division** (*zàn fèn*) corresponding to the **star’s daily position** (*rì suǒ zhàn sù zhī zàn*). Again, double the next **host degree** (*sù dù shù*), add it, and subtract as before.

**Zhōng** (*中*):
- **Nafu** (*孚*) **initial** (*chū*), aligning with **Winter Solstice** (*dōng zhì*) **solar term**, as **yang qi** (*阳气*) begins to generate, and the **sun resides in Qiánniú** (*牵牛*) **initial degree** (*chū dù*), with the **musical pitch** (*lǜ*) centered on **Great Lü** (*Dà Lǚ*).

**Zhōu** (*周*):
- **Next eight** (*fù cì bā*), the **sun resides in Wěinǚ** (*婺女*).

**Lěi** (*礥*):
- **Tún** (*屯*).

**Xián** (*闲*):
- **Tún** (*屯*) **next four** (*cì sì*), **18 fractions** (*shí bā fèn*), **24 seconds** (*èr shí sì miǎo*), marking **Lesser Cold** (*xiǎo hán*), as the **sun progresses to Xuángāo** (*玄枵*), **Dou** (*斗*) **establishes in Chǒu** (*丑*) **position** (*wèi*), and the **pitch** (*lǜ*) is **Great Lü** (*Dà Lǚ*).

**Shǎo** (*少*):
- **Qiān** (*谦*) **five** (*wǔ*), **Xu** (*虚*).

**Lì** (*戾*):
- **Kuì** (*睽*).

**Shàng** (*上*):
- **Ascending seven** (*shēng qī*), **36**, **15** (*shí wǔ*), marking **Greater Cold** (*dà hán*), **seven Wei** (*qī wèi*).

**Gān** (*干*):
- **Ascending** (*shēng*).

**Lín** (*临*).

**Xiàn** (*羡*):
- **Lesser Crossing** (*xiǎo guò*).

- **Lesser Crossing** (*xiǎo guò*), **33**, **22** (*èr shí

**Hànkǎo** (*翰考*):
- **Zhěn-Jiǎo between one degree**, conflicting with *Tàixuān* (*太玄*).

This reckoning is based on the *Han Records* (*《汉志》*).

**Qù** (*去*):
- **Wúwàng** (*无妄*).

- **Gèn** (*艮').

**Chéng** (*成*):

**Xùn** (*驯*):
- **Kūn** (*坤*).

- **Wèijì** (*未济*), **8**, **38**, **Dàxuě** (*大雪*), **Xīngjì** (*星纪*), **Zǐ** (*子*), **Huángzhōng** (*黄钟*).

**Nàn** (*难*):
- **Jiǎn** (*蹇').

**Qín** (*勤*):
- **Jiǎn** (*蹇*).

**Yǎng** (*养*):
- **Yí** (*颐').

**Yǎng** (*养*), **9th cycle’s end**.

The remaining **qi** and **time** total **60 minutes and 24 seconds**.
**Tì** (*踦*) should be **40 minutes and 16 seconds**; **Yíng** (*嬴*) should be **20 minutes and 8 seconds**.

This is the *Tàixuān Calendar* (*《太玄历》*) transmitted by Xu Hán, taken from the *Handwritten Classics* of Wén Gōng. The original author is unspecified.

It is suspected that **Bì** (*贲*) aligns with **Shěn** (*沈*), and **Guān** (*观*) aligns with **Guīmèi** (*归妹*).

In the **Yìmǎo** (*乙卯*) year of the **Hóngzhì** era, in the **12th month**, Xíng Cāncān (*邢参观*) observed this at **Gāoqiáo** (*皋桥*) in **Táng Bóhú’s** (*唐伯虎*) residence.

This copy was formerly kept in **Táng Zǐwèi’s** (*唐子畏*) household, later gifted to **Qián Túnián** (*钱君同爱*). No duplicate exists; it is preserved only through oral transmission. May **Qián Túnián** cherish it.

**Dīngsǐ** (*丁巳*) winter, **Xú Zhēnqīng** (*徐祯卿*) inscribed.

---
**太玄图告卷第十竟**

#1 *Pūshī* (*推*) originally *Wéi* (*惟*), corrected per the main text.
#2 *Chān* (*扦*) originally *Rú* (*杝*), corrected per *Thirteen Classics with Commentaries* (*《十三经注疏》*).

The *Tàixuān Jīng* (*扬子云《太玄经》*) currently available is only **Fàn Wàng’s** (*范望*) *Exegesis* (*《解》*).

Though **Wén Gōng’s** (*温公*) annotated edition had a printed edition during the **Jìngjìng** (*明嘉靖*) era, the text and annotations were printed in large characters, with numerous errors. Moreover, such copies are rare today.

I obtained a shadow-copied **Sòng-dynasty manuscript** from **Qiūtiān Zhāng Jūn** (*秋塘张君*), which was originally housed in **Táng Zǐwèi’s** (*唐子畏*) collection. I thus had it printed, maintaining the original layout. I also requested **Gù Jūn Jiānpíng** (*顾君涧苹*) to re-examine it. Where doubts arose, the original was retained—this was done with utmost caution.

Henceforth, readers of **Yáng Zǐyún’s** (*扬子云*) work who consult **Wén Gōng’s** annotated edition will understand its sources.

**In the 5th month of winter, Gǔwǔ** (*嘉庆*) year **Wùwǔ** (*戊午*), recorded by the **Wǔliǔzhù Zhǔrén** (*五柳居主人*).
